Source Code

These source-code files were obtained by digitally photographing an Artemis 72 (Apollo 15-17 Command Module) program listing from a private collection and then modifying pre-existing Comanche 55 (Apollo 11) source files to incorporate changes. Photography was by Ron Burkey, and transcription was performed by a team of volunteers. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that additional images may be available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 072 OF AGC PROGRAM ARTEMIS 
	BY NASA 2021114-011 11:40 FEB. 26, 1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

001549,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001550,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001551,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     Part of the source code for Artemis (i.e., Colossus 3),
001552,000005:                                                                                                  ##              build 072.  This is for the Command Module's (CM) 
001553,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), for 
001554,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo 15-17.
001555,000008:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001556,000009:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Onno Hommes <ohommes@alumni.cmu.edu>
001557,000010:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
001558,000011:                                                                                                  ## Page Scans:  www.ibiblio.org/apollo/ScansForConversion/Artemis072/
001559,000012:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2009-07-30 OH   Started from corresponding Comanche 055 file.
001560,000013:                                                                                                  ##              2009-11-29 JL   Carried on from where Onno stopped on page 48.
001561,000014:                                                                                                  ##              2010-01-25 JL   Finished conversion.
001562,000015:                                                                                                  ##              2010-01-26 JL   Updated header comments.
001563,000016:                                                                                                  ##              2010-01-31 JL   Fixed build errors.
001564,000017:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-02 JL   Fixed page numbers.
001565,000018:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-02 JL   Fixed ERASE op.
001566,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-09 JL   Fixed addresses of 9X9LOC1 and 9X9LOC2 on p97.
001567,000020:                                                                                                  ##                              Fixed EQUALS on p80.
001568,000021:                                                                                                  ##              2010-02-20 RSB  Un-##'d this header.
001569,000022:                                                                                                  ##              2010-04-12 JL   Fixed tab spacing on a line.
001570,000023:                                                                                                  ##              2011-05-07 JL   Removed workarounds.
001571,000024:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-04 RSB  Proofed comment text using octopus/ProoferComments
001572,000025:                                                                                                  ##                              and fixed errors found.
001573,000026:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-22 RSB  Proofed comment text by diff'ing vs Comanche 55
001574,000027:                                                                                                  ##                              and corrected errors found, though the match between
001575,000028:                                                                                                  ##                              these program versions is not stellar (ha!), so 
001576,000029:                                                                                                  ##                              you shouldn't have too much confidence that all
001577,000030:                                                                                                  ##                              comment-text errors were found. 
001578,000031:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-16 RSB  Comment-text fixes identified in 4-way side-by-side
001579,000032:                                                                                                  ##                              diff of Colossus237/249/Comanche55/Artemis72.
001580,000033:                                                                                                  ##                              Note that there are several instances (marked by 
001581,000034:                                                                                                  ##                              ##-style comments) in which I've added a trailing
001582,000035:                                                                                                  ##                              period not visible in the printout. In these instances
001583,000036:                                                                                                  ##                              I believe that the printout is simply too faint, but 
001584,000037:                                                                                                  ##                              that the periods are really present in the source code.
001585,000038:                                                                                                  ##                              Previously, I had intentionally omitted these periods.
001586,000039:                                                                                                  ##              2021-05-30 ABS  NORMSBIT -> NDRMSBIT
001587,000040:                                                                                                  ##                              GONBYBIT -> G0NBYBIT
001588,000041:                                                                                                  ##                              Removed RUPTSTOR line not present in scans.

Page 38 

001591,000044:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001592,000045: 
001593,000046:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001594,000047:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001595,000048:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001596,000049: 
001597,000050:                                                                                                  #                                        X       EQUALS  START
001598,000051:                                                                                                  #                                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001599,000052:                                                                                                  #                                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001600,000053: 
001601,000054:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001602,000055:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001603,000056:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC,  IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.               )
001604,000057: 
001605,000058: 
001606,000059:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001607,000060:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001608,000061: 
001609,000062:                                                                                                  #                                        X       EQUALS  Y
001610,000063: 
001611,000064: 
001612,000065:                                                                                                  #        = MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001613,000066:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001614,000067: 
001615,000068:                                                                                                  #                                        X       =       Y
001616,000069: 
001617,000070: 
001618,000071:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001619,000072:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001620,000073: 
001621,000074:                                                                                                  #                M REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001622,000075:                                                                                                  #                     B   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001623,000076:                                                                                                  #                         INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001624,000077:                                                                                                  #                     I   MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001625,000078:                                                                                                  #                         INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001626,000079:                                                                                                  #                         INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001627,000080: 
001628,000081:                                                                                                  #                SIZE IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001629,000082: 
001630,000083:                                                                                                  #                N INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001631,000084:                                                                                                  #                     PL MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001632,000085:                                                                                                  #                     DSP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001633,000086:                                                                                                  #                     PRM MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001634,000087:                                                                                                  #                         IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001635,000088:                                                                                                  #                         PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001636,000089:                                                                                                  #                     TMP MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001637,000090:                                                                                                  #                         IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001638,000091:                                                                                                  #                         IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001639,000092:                                                                                                  #                         PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001640,000093:                                                                                                  #                         CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS

Page 39 

001642,000095:                                                                                                  #                         IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001643,000096:                                                                                                  #                         IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001644,000097:                                                                                                  #                     IN  MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001645,000098:                                                                                                  #                         TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001646,000099:                                                                                                  #                     OUT MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001647,000100:                                                                                                  #                         TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001648,000101:

Page 40 

001650,000103: 
001651,000104:                                                                                                  #        SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001652,000105: 
001653,000106: ???????                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001654,000107: ???????                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001655,000108: ???????                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001656,000109: ???????                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001657,000110: ???????                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001658,000111: ???????                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001659,000112: ???????                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001660,000113:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001661,000114: 
001662,000115: ???????                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001663,000116: ???????                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001664,000117: ???????                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001665,000118: ???????                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001666,000119: ???????                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)

The trailing period in the line below is not visible in the printout, but I believe it is simply too faint to see. — RSB 2017.

003319,001772:                                                                                                  #  DESIRES TO BYPASS THE CHANNEL REPRESENTATION, HE SHOULD LOAD C31FLWRD   VIA V21 N01 TO THE VALUES SHOWN IN THE
003320,001773:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING TABLES:
003321,001774: 
003322,001775:                                                                                                  #     A VALUE      MEANING FOR CHANNEL 31                                     B VALUE      MEANING FOR CHANNEL 33
003323,001776: 
003324,001777:                                                                                                  #     0 OR 4       BITS 15,14, + 13 OF CHANNEL 31 ARE VALID                   0 OR 4       BITS 4 + 5 OF CHANNEL 33
003325,001778:                                                                                                  #     1            G&N CONTROL FREE                                           1 OR 5       OPTICS MODE CMC
003326,001779:                                                                                                  #     2            G&N CONTROL ATT. HOLD                                      2 OR 6       OPTICS MODE ZERO
003327,001780:                                                                                                  #     3            G&N CONTROL AUTO                                           3 OR 7       OPTICS MODE MANUAL
003328,001781:                                                                                                  #     5            SCS CONTROL FREE
003329,001782:                                                                                                  #     6            SCS CONTROL ATT. HOLD
